***порадоваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порадоваться.html>пора́доваться</a> (11129)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порадовать.html>пора́довать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porádovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порадоваться.html>пора́доваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porádovatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to rejoice (be happy) for awhile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:порадоваться.html>пора́довались</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>porádovalisʹ</b> i xvátit</i> ― <span class="e-translation">so much for rejoicing</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порадовать.html>пора́довать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porádovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радовать.html>ра́довать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rádovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрадовать.html>обра́довать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obrádovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радоваться.html>ра́доваться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rádovatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрадоваться.html>обра́доваться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obrádovatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***поражать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поражать.html>поража́ть</a> (4813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поражать.html>поража́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poražátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hit, to affect, to strike, to defeat <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to infect or harm</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вирус.html>ви́рус</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гепатит.html>гепати́та</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поражать.html>поража́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клетка.html>кле́тки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печень.html>пе́чени</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vírus gepatíta <b>poražájet</b> klétki péčeni.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Hepatitis virus <b>affects</b> (i.e. infects) the liver cells.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:продолжать.html>продолжа́ли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поражать.html>поража́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:штык.html>штыка́ми</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní prodolžáli <b>poražátʹ</b> protívnika štykámi.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They continued to <b>hit</b> the enemy with bayonets.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to amaze, to strike, to stagger, to startle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поражать.html>поража́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красота.html>красота́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разнообразие.html>разнообра́зие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ших</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зней</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Poražájet</b> krasotá i raznoobrázije nášix žíznej.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The beauty and diversity of our lives <b>is amazing</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***поражение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поражение.html>пораже́ние</a> (2105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Derived from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porazítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to strike, defeat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ение</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-enije</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">noun-forming suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поражение.html>пораже́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poražénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поражение.html>пораже́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поражение.html>пораже́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поражение.html>пораже́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>defeat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>по́лное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поражение.html>пораже́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pólnoje <b>poražénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">utter defeat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потерпеть.html>потерпе́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поражение.html>пораже́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">poterpétʹ <b>poražénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to come off second-best / to suffer a defeat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> deprivation</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> striking, hitting</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> affection, disease</li></ol>

***поразить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ть</a> (1883)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разить.html>рази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porazítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поражать.html>поража́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hit, to affect, to strike, to defeat <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to infect or harm</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вирус.html>ви́рус</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клетка.html>кле́тки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печень.html>пе́чени</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vírus <b>porazíl</b> klétki péčeni.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The virus <b>has affected</b>  (i.e. infected) the liver cells.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>porazítʹ</b> protívnika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to defeat the enemy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to amaze, to strike, to stagger, to startle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красота.html>красото́й</a> кака́я-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщина</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жете</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вспомнить.html>вспо́мнить</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одетый.html>оде́та</a>, - <a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чит</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одетый.html>оде́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идеальный.html>идеа́льно</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jésli vas <b>porazíla</b> krasotój kakája-libo žénščina, no vy ne móžete vspómnitʹ, vo što oná bylá odéta, - znáčit, oná bylá odéta ideálʹno.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">If you <b>are struck</b> by the beauty of a woman but you cannot remember what she was wearing, it means she was dressed perfectly.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***поразиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поразиться.html>порази́ться</a> (8170)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">размы́слить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razmýslitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поранить.html>пора́ненный</a> (22810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поранить.html>пора́ненный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poránennyj</span>)

***поранить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поранить.html>пора́нить</a> (22810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ранить.html>ра́нить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ránitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поранить.html>пора́нить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poránitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wound, to injure, to hurt <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually not severely</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водитель.html>води́телю</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поранить.html>пора́нило</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vodítelju <b>poránilo</b> rúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the driver <b>hurt</b> his hand</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поране́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poranénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поране́нье</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poranénʹje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порасти.html>порасти́</a> (8303)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расти.html>расти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***порвать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порвать.html>порва́ть</a> (5752)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порвать.html>порва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tear (rend)</li>
<li>to tear apart
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неисправный.html>неиспра́вный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:принтер.html>при́нтер</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порвать.html>порва́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печатать.html>печа́тал</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Neisprávnyj príntɛr tólʹko <b>porvál</b> bumágu i ničevó ne pečátal.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The broken printer only <b>tore</b> the paper <b>apart</b> and didn't print anything.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tear out</li>
<li>to break off (a relationship)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">порыва́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to break with <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> someone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порвать.html>порва́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уехать.html>уе́хал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> далёкий <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>porvál</b> so vsem i ujéxal v daljókij górod.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>broke with</b> everything and left for a faraway town.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">порыва́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порвать.html>порва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***порекомендовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порекомендовать.html>порекомендова́ть</a> (18547)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***порешить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порешить.html>пореши́ть</a> (13370)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:решить.html>реши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rešítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порешить.html>пореши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porešítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to decide, to settle <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порешить.html>пореши́ли</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na tom i <b>porešíli</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">they settled on that</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чём</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порешить.html>пореши́м</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tak na čóm <b>poreším</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">so what shall we decide [settle on]?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to finish off, to do away <i>(with)</i></li></ol>

***порицание.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порицание.html>порица́ние</a> (28263)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">порица́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poricátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порицание.html>порица́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poricánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порицание.html>порица́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порицание.html>порица́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порицание.html>порица́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>censure, animadversion <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">criticism, a critical remark</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>blame, reprobation</li>
<li>reproof, reproval, reprehension</li>
<li>reflection, reflexion</li>
<li>dispraise</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фия</a> (20380)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pornográfija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pornography
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́вится</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жестокий.html>жесто́кая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фия</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú nrávitsja žestókaja <b>pornográfija</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He likes violent pornography.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ла</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мает</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фия</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:унижать.html>унижа́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщин</a>. «<a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голуба́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фия</a></b>?» — <a href = vnd.unilang:спросить.html>спроси́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́довало</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ожидать.html>ожида́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:промолчать.html>промолча́ла</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná skazála, što dúmajet, što <b>pornográfija</b> unižájet žénščin. “A kak že golubája <b>pornográfija</b>?” — sprosíl ja. Kak i slédovalo ožidátʹ, oná promolčála.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She said that she thinks pornography degrades women. "What about gay porn?" I asked. Unsurprisingly, she remained silent.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
